class="cl-964e8d20">experienced</span><span class="cl-964e8d20"> </span><span class="cl-964e8d20">a</span><span class="cl-964e8d20"> </span><span class="cl-964e8d34">end</span><span class="cl-964e8d34"> </span><span class="cl-964e8d34">of</span><span class="cl-964e8d34"> </span><span class="cl-964e8d34">crisis</span><span class="cl-964e8d20">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-964ec588"><p class="cl-964e9996"><span class="cl-964e8d20">226.12</span></p></td><td class="cl-964ec57e"><p class="cl-964e9996"><span class="cl-964e8d20">UN activity took the form of a discussion in the Security Council; no resolution was passed.</span></p></td><td class="cl-964ec57e"><p class="cl-964e9996"><span class="cl-964e8d34">United</span><span class="cl-964e8d34"> </span><span class="cl-964e8d34">Nations</span><span class="cl-964e8d20"> </span><span class="cl-964e8d20">initiated</span><span politically active in this crisis, with little effect.</span></p></td><td class="cl-964ec589"><p class="cl-964e9996"><span class="cl-964e8d20">No</span><span class="cl-964e8d20"> </span><span and political conflict within the Czechoslovak Communist Party led to the overthrow of Antonin Novotny as First Secretary of the Communist Party on 5 January 1968 and as the State President on 23 March 1968.</span></p></td><td class="cl-96584dc4"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">No</span><span class="cl-9657ff0e"> </span><span class="cl-9657ff0e">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr class="cl-96584dce"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">No</span><span class="cl-9657ff0e"> </span><span class="cl-9657ff0e">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr </span><span class="cl-9657ff0e">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-96584dcf"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">227.6</span></p></td><td class="cl-96584dce"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">economic crisis, the Slovak question, the rehabilitation of party leaders sentenced during the purges of the 1950s, and a way to deal with the dissent of students and intellectuals.</span></p></td><td class="cl-96584dce"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">No</span><span class="cl-9657ff0e"> </span><span class="cl-96584dc4"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">Censorship was abolished, economic controls and central planning by the government were reduced and restructured, and new members were appointed to political posts.</span></p></td><td class="cl-96584dc4"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">No</span><span class="cl-9657ff0e"> </span><span and the USSR in particular.</span></p></td><td class="cl-96584dce"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">No</span><span class="cl-9657ff0e"> </span><span early stages in their countries, would spread and undermine their respective positions.</span></p></td><td class="cl-96584dc4"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">No</span><span Ukrainian nationalist sentiment; and the possibility emerged that liberalization would spill over into neighboring states.</span></p></td><td class="cl-96584dce"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span </span><span class="cl-9657ff0e">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-96584dc5"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">227.13</span></p></td><td for East Germany and Poland.</span></p></td><td class="cl-96584dc4"><p class="cl-96580c92"><span class="cl-9657ff0e">No</span><span class="cl-9657ff0e"> </span><span operate as a "state within a state" in Lebanon.</span></p></td><td class="cl-96b03c46"><p class="cl-96b017de"><span class="cl-96b00c30">No</span><span class="cl-96b00c30"> </span><span class="cl-96b00c30">events.</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
